# Integrands of the form x^(k n-1) (a+b x^n)^(p/2)

# p>0
[x^(-1+4*n)*(a+b*x^n)^(1/2),x,3,-2/3*a^3*(a+b*x^n)^(3/2)/(b^4*n)+6/5*a^2*(a+b*x^n)^(5/2)/(b^4*n)-6/7*a*(a+b*x^n)^(7/2)/(b^4*n)+2/9*(a+b*x^n)^(9/2)/(b^4*n)],

# Integrands of the form x^m (a+b x^n)^p with m symbolic

[x^(-1-1/2*n)/sqrt(a+b*x^n),x,1,-2*sqrt(a+b*x^n)/(a*n*x^(1/2*n))],

[a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n),x,3,a*x+1/2*b*x*(c*x^n)^(1/n)],
[(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^2,x,2,1/3*x*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^3/(b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))],
[(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^3,x,2,1/4*x*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^4/(b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))],

# p<0
[x^3/(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)),x,3,a^2*x^4/(b^3*(c*x^n)^(3/n))-1/2*a*x^4/(b^2*(c*x^n)^(2/n))+1/3*x^4/(b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))-a^3*x^4*log(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(b^4*(c*x^n)^(4/n))],
[x^2/(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)),x,3,-a*x^3/(b^2*(c*x^n)^(2/n))+1/2*x^3/(b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))+a^2*x^3*log(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(b^3*(c*x^n)^(3/n))],
[x/(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)),x,3,x^2/(b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))-a*x^2*log(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(b^2*(c*x^n)^(2/n))],
[1/(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)),x,2,x*log(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))],
[1/(x*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))),x,4,log(x)/a-log(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/a],
[1/(x^2*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))),x,3,(-1)/(a*x)-b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)*log(x)/(a^2*x)+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)*log(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(a^2*x)],
[1/(x^3*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))),x,3,(-1/2)/(a*x^2)+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)/(a^2*x^2)+b^2*(c*x^n)^(2/n)*log(x)/(a^3*x^2)-b^2*(c*x^n)^(2/n)*log(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(a^3*x^2)],
[x^3/(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^2,x,3,-2*a*x^4/(b^3*(c*x^n)^(3/n))+1/2*x^4/(b^2*(c*x^n)^(2/n))+a^3*x^4/(b^4*(c*x^n)^(4/n)*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)))+3*a^2*x^4*log(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(b^4*(c*x^n)^(4/n))],
[x^2/(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^2,x,3,x^3/(b^2*(c*x^n)^(2/n))-a^2*x^3/(b^3*(c*x^n)^(3/n)*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)))-2*a*x^3*log(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(b^3*(c*x^n)^(3/n))],
[x/(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^2,x,3,a*x^2/(b^2*(c*x^n)^(2/n)*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)))+x^2*log(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(b^2*(c*x^n)^(2/n))],
[1/(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^2,x,2,x/(a^2+a*b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)),-x/(b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)))],
[1/(x*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^2),x,3,1/(a*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)))+log(x)/a^2-log(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/a^2],
[1/(x^2*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^2),x,3,(-1)/(a^2*x)-b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)/(a^2*x*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)))-2*b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)*log(x)/(a^3*x)+2*b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)*log(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(a^3*x)],
[1/(x^3*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^2),x,3,(-1/2)/(a^2*x^2)+2*b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)/(a^3*x^2)+b^2*(c*x^n)^(2/n)/(a^3*x^2*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)))+3*b^2*(c*x^n)^(2/n)*log(x)/(a^4*x^2)-3*b^2*(c*x^n)^(2/n)*log(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(a^4*x^2)],
[1/(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^3,x,2,-1/2*x/(b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^2)],
[x/(1+(x^n)^(1/n))^2,x,3,x^2/((x^n)^(2/n)*(1+(x^n)^(1/n)))+x^2*log(1+(x^n)^(1/n))/(x^n)^(2/n)],

# p symbolic
[x^3*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^p,x,3,-a^3*x^4*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^(1+p)/(b^4*(1+p)*(c*x^n)^(4/n))+3*a^2*x^4*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^(2+p)/(b^4*(2+p)*(c*x^n)^(4/n))-3*a*x^4*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^(3+p)/(b^4*(3+p)*(c*x^n)^(4/n))+x^4*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^(4+p)/(b^4*(4+p)*(c*x^n)^(4/n))],
[x^2*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^p,x,3,a^2*x^3*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^(1+p)/(b^3*(1+p)*(c*x^n)^(3/n))-2*a*x^3*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^(2+p)/(b^3*(2+p)*(c*x^n)^(3/n))+x^3*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^(3+p)/(b^3*(3+p)*(c*x^n)^(3/n))],
[x*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^p,x,3,-a*x^2*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^(1+p)/(b^2*(1+p)*(c*x^n)^(2/n))+x^2*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^(2+p)/(b^2*(2+p)*(c*x^n)^(2/n))],
[(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^p,x,2,x*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^(1+p)/(b*(1+p)*(c*x^n)^(1/n))],
[(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^p/x,x,2,-(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^(1+p)*hypergeom([1,1+p],[2+p],1+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)/a)/(a*(1+p))],
[(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^p/x^2,x,2,b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n))^(1+p)*hypergeom([2,1+p],[2+p],1+b*(c*x^n)^(1/n)/a)/(a^2*(1+p)*x)],

# Integrands of the form x^m (a+b (c x^n)^(2/n))^p
[(a+b*(c*x^n)^(2/n))^3,x,3,a^3*x+a^2*b*x*(c*x^n)^(2/n)+3/5*a*b^2*x*(c*x^n)^(4/n)+1/7*b^3*x*(c*x^n)^(6/n)],
[(a+b*(c*x^n)^(2/n))^2,x,3,a^2*x+2/3*a*b*x*(c*x^n)^(2/n)+1/5*b^2*x*(c*x^n)^(4/n)],
[a+b*(c*x^n)^(2/n),x,3,a*x+1/3*b*x*(c*x^n)^(2/n)],
[1/(a+b*(c*x^n)^(2/n)),x,2,x*arctan((c*x^n)^(1/n)*sqrt(b)/sqrt(a))/((c*x^n)^(1/n)*sqrt(a)*sqrt(b))],
[1/(a+b*(c*x^n)^(2/n))^2,x,3,1/2*x/(a*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(2/n)))+1/2*x*arctan((c*x^n)^(1/n)*sqrt(b)/sqrt(a))/(a^(3/2)*(c*x^n)^(1/n)*sqrt(b))],
[1/(a+b*(c*x^n)^(2/n))^3,x,4,1/4*x/(a*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(2/n))^2)+3/8*x/(a^2*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(2/n)))+3/8*x*arctan((c*x^n)^(1/n)*sqrt(b)/sqrt(a))/(a^(5/2)*(c*x^n)^(1/n)*sqrt(b))],
[1/(1+4*sqrt(x^4)),x,2,1/2*x*arctan(2*(x^4)^(1/4))/(x^4)^(1/4)],
[1/(1-4*sqrt(x^4)),x,2,1/2*x*arctanh(2*(x^4)^(1/4))/(x^4)^(1/4)],
[1/(1+4*(x^6)^(1/3)),x,2,1/2*x*arctan(2*(x^6)^(1/6))/(x^6)^(1/6)],
[1/(1-4*(x^6)^(1/3)),x,2,1/2*x*arctanh(2*(x^6)^(1/6))/(x^6)^(1/6)],
[1/(1+4*(x^(2*n))^(1/n)),x,2,1/2*x*arctan(2*(x^(2*n))^(1/2/n))/(x^(2*n))^(1/2/n)],
[1/(1-4*(x^(2*n))^(1/n)),x,2,1/2*x*arctanh(2*(x^(2*n))^(1/2/n))/(x^(2*n))^(1/2/n)],

# Integrands of the form x^m (a+b (c x^n)^(3/n))^p
[(a+b*(c*x^n)^(3/n))^3,x,3,a^3*x+3/4*a^2*b*x*(c*x^n)^(3/n)+3/7*a*b^2*x*(c*x^n)^(6/n)+1/10*b^3*x*(c*x^n)^(9/n)],
[(a+b*(c*x^n)^(3/n))^2,x,3,a^2*x+1/2*a*b*x*(c*x^n)^(3/n)+1/7*b^2*x*(c*x^n)^(6/n)],
[a+b*(c*x^n)^(3/n),x,3,a*x+1/4*b*x*(c*x^n)^(3/n)],
[1/(a+b*(c*x^n)^(3/n)),x,7,1/3*x*log(a^(1/3)+b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(a^(2/3)*b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n))-1/6*x*log(a^(2/3)-a^(1/3)*b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n)+b^(2/3)*(c*x^n)^(2/n))/(a^(2/3)*b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n))-x*arctan((a^(1/3)-2*b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(a^(1/3)*sqrt(3)))/(a^(2/3)*b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n)*sqrt(3))],
[1/(a+b*(c*x^n)^(3/n))^2,x,8,1/3*x/(a*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(3/n)))+2/9*x*log(a^(1/3)+b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(a^(5/3)*b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n))-1/9*x*log(a^(2/3)-a^(1/3)*b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n)+b^(2/3)*(c*x^n)^(2/n))/(a^(5/3)*b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n))-2/3*x*arctan((a^(1/3)-2*b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(a^(1/3)*sqrt(3)))/(a^(5/3)*b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n)*sqrt(3))],
[1/(a+b*(c*x^n)^(3/n))^3,x,9,1/6*x/(a*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(3/n))^2)+5/18*x/(a^2*(a+b*(c*x^n)^(3/n)))+5/27*x*log(a^(1/3)+b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(a^(8/3)*b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n))-5/54*x*log(a^(2/3)-a^(1/3)*b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n)+b^(2/3)*(c*x^n)^(2/n))/(a^(8/3)*b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n))-5/9*x*arctan((a^(1/3)-2*b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n))/(a^(1/3)*sqrt(3)))/(a^(8/3)*b^(1/3)*(c*x^n)^(1/n)*sqrt(3))],

# Integrands of the form (d x)^m (a+b (c x^q)^n)^p with n, p and q symbolic
[(d*x)^m*(a+b*(c*x^q)^n)^p,x,3,(d*x)^(1+m)*(a+b*(c*x^q)^n)^p*hypergeom([-p,(1+m)/(n*q)],[1+(1+m)/(n*q)],-b*(c*x^q)^n/a)/(d*(1+m)*(1+b*(c*x^q)^n/a)^p)],
[x^2*(a+b*(c*x^q)^n)^p,x,3,1/3*x^3*(a+b*(c*x^q)^n)^p*hypergeom([-p,3/(n*q)],[1+3/(n*q)],-b*(c*x^q)^n/a)/(1+b*(c*x^q)^n/a)^p],
[x*(a+b*(c*x^q)^n)^p,x,3,1/2*x^2*(a+b*(c*x^q)^n)^p*hypergeom([-p,2/(n*q)],[1+2/(n*q)],-b*(c*x^q)^n/a)/(1+b*(c*x^q)^n/a)^p],
[(a+b*(c*x^q)^n)^p,x,3,x*(a+b*(c*x^q)^n)^p*hypergeom([-p,1/(n*q)],[1+1/(n*q)],-b*(c*x^q)^n/a)/(1+b*(c*x^q)^n/a)^p],
[(a+b*(c*x^q)^n)^p/x,x,3,-(a+b*(c*x^q)^n)^(1+p)*hypergeom([1,1+p],[2+p],1+b*(c*x^q)^n/a)/(a*n*(1+p)*q)],
[(a+b*(c*x^q)^n)^p/x^2,x,3,-(a+b*(c*x^q)^n)^p*hypergeom([-p,(-1)/(n*q)],[1+(-1)/(n*q)],-b*(c*x^q)^n/a)/(x*(1+b*(c*x^q)^n/a)^p)],

# Integrands of the form x^m (a+b (d/x)^n+c (d/x)^(2n))^p
[x^m*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x)),x,4,x^(1+m)*AppellF1(-2*(1+m),-1/2,-1/2,-1-2*m,-2*c*sqrt(d/x)/(sqrt(d)*(b*sqrt(d)-sqrt(-4*a*c+b^2*d))),-2*c*sqrt(d/x)/(sqrt(d)*(b*sqrt(d)+sqrt(-4*a*c+b^2*d))))*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/((1+m)*sqrt(1+2*c*sqrt(d/x)/(sqrt(d)*(b*sqrt(d)-sqrt(-4*a*c+b^2*d))))*sqrt(1+2*c*sqrt(d/x)/(sqrt(d)*(b*sqrt(d)+sqrt(-4*a*c+b^2*d)))))],
[x^2*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x)),x,9,1/512*(4*a*c-b^2*d)*(16*a^2*c^2-56*a*b^2*c*d+21*b^4*d^2)*arctanh(1/2*(2*a+b*sqrt(d/x))/(sqrt(a)*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))))/a^(11/2)-3/10*b*d^3*(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))^(3/2)/(a^2*(d/x)^(5/2))+7/480*b*d^2*(28*a*c-15*b^2*d)*(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))^(3/2)/(a^4*(d/x)^(3/2))-1/80*(20*a*c-21*b^2*d)*x^2*(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))^(3/2)/a^3+1/3*x^3*(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))^(3/2)/a+1/256*(16*a^2*c^2-56*a*b^2*c*d+21*b^4*d^2)*x*(2*a+b*sqrt(d/x))*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/a^5],
[x*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x)),x,7,-1/64*(4*a*c-5*b^2*d)*(4*a*c-b^2*d)*arctanh(1/2*(2*a+b*sqrt(d/x))/(sqrt(a)*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))))/a^(7/2)-5/12*b*d^2*(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))^(3/2)/(a^2*(d/x)^(3/2))+1/2*x^2*(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))^(3/2)/a-1/32*(4*a*c-5*b^2*d)*x*(2*a+b*sqrt(d/x))*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/a^3],
[sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x)),x,5,1/4*(4*a*c-b^2*d)*arctanh(1/2*(2*a+b*sqrt(d/x))/(sqrt(a)*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))))/a^(3/2)+1/2*x*(2*a+b*sqrt(d/x))*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/a],
[sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/x,x,8,2*arctanh(1/2*(2*a+b*sqrt(d/x))/(sqrt(a)*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))))*sqrt(a)-b*arctanh(1/2*(b*d+2*c*sqrt(d/x))/(sqrt(c)*sqrt(d)*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))))*sqrt(d)/sqrt(c)-2*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))],
[sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/x^2,x,6,1/8*b*(4*a*c-b^2*d)*arctanh(1/2*(b*d+2*c*sqrt(d/x))/(sqrt(c)*sqrt(d)*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))))*sqrt(d)/c^(5/2)-2/3*(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))^(3/2)/c+1/4*b*(b*d+2*c*sqrt(d/x))*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/c^2],
[sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/x^3,x,7,-1/128*b*(12*a*c-7*b^2*d)*(4*a*c-b^2*d)*arctanh(1/2*(b*d+2*c*sqrt(d/x))/(sqrt(c)*sqrt(d)*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))))*sqrt(d)/c^(9/2)-2/5*(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))^(3/2)/(c*x)+1/120*(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))^(3/2)*(32*a*c-35*b^2*d+42*b*c*sqrt(d/x))/c^3-1/64*b*(12*a*c-7*b^2*d)*(b*d+2*c*sqrt(d/x))*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/c^4],
[sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/x^4,x,9,1/1024*b*(4*a*c-b^2*d)*(80*a^2*c^2-120*a*b^2*c*d+33*b^4*d^2)*arctanh(1/2*(b*d+2*c*sqrt(d/x))/(sqrt(c)*sqrt(d)*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))))*sqrt(d)/c^(13/2)+11/42*b*(d/x)^(3/2)*(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))^(3/2)/(c^2*d)-2/7*(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))^(3/2)/(c*x^2)+1/140*(32*a*c-33*b^2*d)*(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))^(3/2)/(c^3*x)-1/6720*(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))^(3/2)*(1024*a^2*c^2-3276*a*b^2*c*d+1155*b^4*d^2+18*b*c*(148*a*c-77*b^2*d)*sqrt(d/x))/c^5+1/512*b*(80*a^2*c^2-120*a*b^2*c*d+33*b^4*d^2)*(b*d+2*c*sqrt(d/x))*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/c^6],
[x^m/sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x)),x,4,x^(1+m)*AppellF1(-2*(1+m),1/2,1/2,-1-2*m,-2*c*sqrt(d/x)/(sqrt(d)*(b*sqrt(d)-sqrt(-4*a*c+b^2*d))),-2*c*sqrt(d/x)/(sqrt(d)*(b*sqrt(d)+sqrt(-4*a*c+b^2*d))))*sqrt(1+2*c*sqrt(d/x)/(sqrt(d)*(b*sqrt(d)-sqrt(-4*a*c+b^2*d))))*sqrt(1+2*c*sqrt(d/x)/(sqrt(d)*(b*sqrt(d)+sqrt(-4*a*c+b^2*d))))/((1+m)*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x)))],
[x^2/sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x)),x,10,-1/512*(320*a^3*c^3-1680*a^2*b^2*c^2*d+1260*a*b^4*c*d^2-231*b^6*d^3)*arctanh(1/2*(2*a+b*sqrt(d/x))/(sqrt(a)*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))))/a^(13/2)-11/30*b*d^3*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/(a^2*(d/x)^(5/2))+1/160*b*d^2*(156*a*c-77*b^2*d)*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/(a^4*(d/x)^(3/2))+1/640*(400*a^2*c^2-1176*a*b^2*c*d+385*b^4*d^2)*x*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/a^5-1/240*(100*a*c-99*b^2*d)*x^2*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/a^3+1/3*x^3*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/a-7/1280*b*d*(528*a^2*c^2-680*a*b^2*c*d+165*b^4*d^2)*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/(a^6*sqrt(d/x))],
[x/sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x)),x,8,1/64*(48*a^2*c^2-120*a*b^2*c*d+35*b^4*d^2)*arctanh(1/2*(2*a+b*sqrt(d/x))/(sqrt(a)*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))))/a^(9/2)-7/12*b*d^2*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/(a^2*(d/x)^(3/2))-1/48*(36*a*c-35*b^2*d)*x*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/a^3+1/2*x^2*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/a+5/96*b*d*(44*a*c-21*b^2*d)*sqrt(a+c/x+b*sqrt(d/x))/(a^4*sqrt(d/x))],

# Integrands of the form (c x^n)^(1/n) (a+b (c x^n)^(m/n))^p
